The executive suite is really not as good as the ordinary guest room. With this money, it is better to go directly to the Sheraton Seaside.
When checking in, they said that the soft drinks in the refrigerator can be drunk for free. When checking out, the front desk asked me if I had drunk them. I said that they told me that they were all free the day before, and they confirmed with me who said that and then slumped.
The door lock was still broken, and I couldn't lock the door at all. The next morning at 9:30, I fell asleep and heard someone open the door, open and close it. How could they open the door so casually? Didn't they know someone was staying there? I didn't call room service, so why didn't they clean the room more if they could open the door so casually?
